reduction was very high, about 50%, which again is caused by the large initial
dimensions.
When comparing the result with the ones obtained in Table 7.10, it is observed
that the result doesn't correspond exactly to each other. The results from the
combined optimization is lower than the ones from the fatigue optimization. It
is primarily the dimensions of the ribs, which diers between the models, i.e.
ts and tp is lowest for the combined model. This shows that the optimization
for fatigue has an inuence on the optimization in the combined optimization
program, which is a little unexpected considering the results from section 7.3.
Because only one analysis is performed, lack of results and informations to see if
the results for the giving initial guess was a yer or if the optimization program
is working as intended. Therefore, more analyzes have to be performed in order
to make a nal conclusion for whether or not the combined optimization program
for the stiened plate is working as intended.
==PAGE:97==
Chapter 9
Discussion
Throughout this project several optimization programs where developed. The
programs were built up by using the programs: matlab as the optimization
algorithm, python as a storage of the FE model information and abaqus as
calculator for the FE analysis.
To begin with the connection between the three programs were established by
optimising a cantilever beam. There were no problems connection the three
programs, however the optimization using abaqus wasn't corresponding to an
analytical approach. It turned out that the input le to the analysis in abaqus
was only containing 6 digits for cross-section dimensions, i.e. thickness, width,
height ect. This can cause problems for the optimization algorithm in matlab,
because the algorithm is changing dimensions in a relative size of the numbers.
For a structure with large dierences between the dimensions, which are opti-
mized, the algorithm may not nd the correct solution, because the change in
the dimensions are so small to have an inuence on the calculations in abaqus.
This was also the case for the optimization of the cantilever beam. The problem
was handled by changing the minimum size of the change of the dimensions.
Another way can be to chose more convenient units such as cm or mm instead
of meters. The only way to solve the problem is to write the input le (inp-le)
self.
By changing the minimum size of the change in the optimization algorithm, it
was possible to make an optimization program for the cantilever beam by using
the two minimization algorithms fminsearch and fmincon. Both optimization
programs showed almost no deviation from abaqus and an analytical approach.
The original idea was to make an optimization program for a plate with ribs
based on a top plate from Izmit Bay Bridge. However the closed trapezoidal
ribs from Izmit Bay Bridge was changed to opened plate ribs. This was done
==PAGE:98==
84
Discussion
because the complexity of the trapezoidal ribs, and because the optimization
program is meant to be a principle program to show that it is possible to make
an optimization program using matlab, python and abaqus for long span
bridges. The change of the ribs made the comparison between the dimensions
found in the analysis and the dimensions of Izmit Bay Bridge more dicult.
When making the FE model of the stiened plate several assumptions were
made.
The boundary conditions in both the longitudinal and transverse di-
rections where simplied. It was assumed that the diaphragms in the bridge
was acting as simple supports for the plate in the longitudinal direction, which
doesn't imply enough stiness to the structure. Also the rods in the bridge
deck was assumed to act as simple supports in the transverse direction. This is
also not corresponding to the reality. These boundary conditions are not giving
enough sti to the FE model compared to the real bridge and the results will
therefore deviate from the Izmit Bay Bridge.
The optimization program for stability showed acceptable results. The program
optimized the structure compared to the initial dimensions, and they where in an
acceptable range of the dimensions of Izmit Bay Bridge, even with the changes
in geometry and simplications of the FE model. The results also showed that
dierent initial dimensions would result in dierent optimized dimensions. This
could be caused by the algorithm nding local minimum points and therefore
not nd the most optimal solution. The local minimum points could indicate
that the FE model takes dynamical plate behaviour into account. It is therefore
a wise idea to make several initial guess of the dimensions when running the
optimization program.
The results from the fatigue optimization program was not as expected. Or-
thotropic bridges are typically designed based on the fatigue stresses however,
the optimization results converged to the lower bounds of the algorithm.
It
turned out that the stresses changed in magnitude and from compression to
tension and vise versa when the dimensions of the thickness of the plate, the
thickness of the stieners and height of the stieners changed. This was a prob-
lem because of the method used to extract the stresses. The stresses where
extracted from one specic node, and when the stresses were changing, the
node didn't contain the largest stress any longer. This caused the optimization
program to get unwanted results. This could be indicating that something is
wrong with the model, or that the method of extracting the results are inappro-
priate. The method to extract the results are denitely not the must eective
or optimal way of doing it. Therefore, a more reliable method of extracting the
results is needed.
A suggestion for a method of extracting the stress is to take the largest stress
for the whole model for all calculations, the problem with this method is, that
it isn't certain that the maximum stress is at a connection between the plate
and a stiener. Another suggestion could be to make the material orientation
==PAGE:99==
85
the same for both plate and stieners, this was attempted in section 7.3 but
without any success.
Furthermore, shell elements were used in the FE model. Beam elements would
properly have been preferred, since the plate is load perpendicular to its plane.
This can be taken into consideration for further analysis.
At last an optimization program combining stability and fatigue was made. It
was dicult to conclude anything from the analysis, because only one result were
obtained. However the result showed that the fatigue analysis had an inuence
on the optimization. This was unexpected since it for its own analysis converged
to the lower bounds of the algorithm.
This has to be further investigated,
but it shows that it is possible to make an optimization program with several
constrains.
==PAGE:100==
86
Discussion
==PAGE:101==
Chapter 10
Conclusion
Based on the analyzes made throughout this project, it is concluded that it
is possible to make an optimization program for atleast the stability of an or-
thtropic steel deck using the three programs matlab, python and abaqus.
matlab is used to manage the optimization by running the optimization algo-
rithm, python used as a storage of the FE model information and abaqus was
used as calculator for the FE analysis. However it wasn't possible to optimize
for fatigue.
The analysis for the stability optimization showed that the program optimized
the structure with respect to the volume (material usage). The structure were
also optimized in comparison to the reference model (Izmit Bay Bridge), even
though many simplications were made and a lot of stiness was removed from
the structure due to changing of the rib system and boundary conditions. The
results showed that local minimum points where found for dierent initial di-
mensions.
This indicates that the FE model is taken the ratio between the
length and width of the plates into account.
The analysis for the fatigue however, showed that there were problems with the
analysis and unexpected results were obtained. The reason for the unexpected
results were caused by the changes in the stresses in the plate when changing
the dimensions of the plate thickness, the thickness of the stieners and the
height of the stieners. The changes made the hot spot change places in the
plate, which made it impossible to get a proper results, because the algorithm
converged to the lower bound.
==PAGE:102==
88
Conclusion
Also a combined optimization program for stability and fatigue was developed.
The program optimized the structure compared to the initial structure and Izmit
Bay Bridge. The results were almost the same as for the stability optimization
because of the problems with the fatigue model.
However, the optimization
program showed that could be capable of optimizing for two constrains.
If a solution to the problems in the fatigue optimization is solved, the optimiza-
tion program will most likely be capable to optimize the bridge deck of Izmit
Bay Bridge. Also future othotropic bridges can be optimized before construc-
tion, which could result in longer main span for the bridges and reduction of
material used. However, the FE models need to be more detailed, than the ones
in this project.
==PAGE:103==
Chapter 11
Further work
The future work with the optimization program will primarily be to improve
the model for the fatigue analysis and to make it work properly. When the
optimization program for fatigue is working the next step is to make a combined
optimization program for both stability and fatigue.
A proposal was made
in the project, which should be working when the optimization for fatigue is
working. However, an investigation has to be made to insure that the combined
optimization program is working properly.
Furthermore, the optimization program for the Izmit Bay Bridge can be further
developed by improving the FE models. The models had a lot of simplications
and the extraction of stresses in the fatigue analysis wasn't performed the most
optimal way. This is the major points where the optimization program can be
develop on.
To be able to compare the results with the Izmit Bay Bridge, the geometry of
the rib system has to be changed to a trapezoidal closed system. This will make
the FE model more complex. This will also make the optimization program
more relevant for other bridges since the closed trapezoidal rib systems are used
for the bridges with the longest main spans. Also an extension of the FE model
to contain more than a single top plate can improve the program.
The optimization algorithm itself is dicult to optimize.
A possibility is to
change the minimization algorithm to one of the other built-in algorithm in
matlab or to develop one.

function u = Ana(h1 , h , a , t ,E,P)

that

5

of

6

[m3]

the
midtpoint
of

11
% M = p∗a ;

i n e r t i a
for

part
[m4]

[m]

1
function
[ c , ceq ] = Aba(x , L,w, db , ws , ds , nribs ,E,A0, PStab ,

% A function
that
c a l c u l a t e s
the

of a
3
%

4
% The function

6

in

the
cross−section
9
10
%% Make a python

==PAGE:195==
Appendix G
Mesh convergence of
cantilever beam
For the FE model of the cantilever beam a check of the mesh convergence is
performed. The convergence check is performed by increasing the number of
elements in each part of the beam and compare the displacement with the num-
ber of elements. The elements used are high order elements B23. In Figure G.1
the displacement as function of the number of elements are plotted.
Figure G.1: Mesh convergence of the cantilever beam.
It is seen that the displacement is already converged at one element per part.
Because the analysis is quick, it is chosen to use ve elements per part.
==PAGE:196==
86
Mesh convergence of cantilever beam
==PAGE:197==
Appendix H
Mesh convergence of plate
for stability
For the FE model of the plate a not adequate mesh convergence check is per-
formed. This is only used to show how the mesh convergence check is performed,
but a more in depth investigating needs to be performed. The elements are
STRI65. In Figure H.1 the eigenvalue as function of the number of elements are
plotted.
Figure H.1: Mesh convergence of plate in the longitudinal direction.
It is seen that the eigenvalue is converged at around 3200 elements, which cor-
respond to a element size of L/20 in the longitudinal direction. This will be the
meshed used in the model.
==PAGE:198==
88
Mesh convergence of plate for stability
